           <div class="single-product-title"> 
            <h1 itemprop="name" class="product_title entry-title">Multivendor E-commerce Store</h1> 
            <div class="product-brand"></div> 
           </div> 
           <div class="product-action-buttons"> 
           </div>
           <!-- /.product-action-buttons --> 
           <div itemprop="description"> 
            <p>In this business world everyone prefers to do online shopping in order to make their shopping easily because it consumes time. PHP scripts mall implemented the readymade <strong>Multivendor Ecommerce script</strong>. Let the vendors sign up at your store and they can organize their own products and sales in a common marketplace website. You can have unlimited number of vendors at your store and you can expand more and more independent vendors. </p> 
            <p>The products from different independent vendors will appear at your website and the users can do shopping at your website. In <strong>Open Source Multi Vendor Shopping Cart Script</strong>, each vendor can manage their own admin panel and customize the products and settings according their desire. Vendors do not interact or interfere with each other products and sales. &nbsp;The root administrator can have full control of the products listings, sales and transactions.</p> 
            <p><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p> 
            <p><a class="le-button huge" style="-webkit-transition: all 0.2s ease-out 0s; transition: all 0.2s ease-out 0s; min-height: 0px; min-width: 0px; line-height: 16px; border-width: 0px; margin: 0px; padding: 15px 43px; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 12px;" href="http://74.124.215.220/~bizquest/demo/ecomm/" target="_blank">User Demo</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="margin-left:10px; margin-right: 25px;"><a class="le-button huge" style="-webkit-transition: all 0.2s ease-out 0s; transition: all 0.2s ease-out 0s; min-height: 0px; min-width: 0px; line-height: 16px; border-width: 0px; margin: 0px; padding: 15px 43px; letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 12px;" href="http://www.phpscriptsmall.com/documents/multivendor-document.docx" target="_blank">Download Document</a></span></p> 
           </div>

         <div class="panel entry-content wc-tab" id="tab-description"> 
          <h2>Product Description</h2> 
          <p>The transaction happens between the root admin and the one who purchase the product. Finally the payments are distributed to each vendor based on the product sold through the admin. All the vendors can manage their own records of products sold and transaction for each product.</p> 
          <p>You can set your own commission rates and auctions for the products displayed. The script is highly customizable where you can modify the homepage banners, categories, email ids, contact details and other necessary informations. The script has responsive page layouts and it suits all the screens. Best <strong>Multi Vendor PHP Solution</strong> supports numerous products such like accessories, gadgets, home appliances etc. &nbsp;The script has user friendly navigations and highly secured codes.</p> 
          <p>We have 12 years of experience in this e-commerce field and striving to satisfy all the needs of the customers to make them easy go steps. We have SEO friendly concept. We provide free technical support for the next 1 year once you purchase our script. We also provide free updates for 6 months and you are not supposed to search and run for improvisation for your website. We also provide brand free and free installation.</p> 
          <p><strong>Please check our other PHP E-Commerce Scripts <a href="http://www.phpscriptsmall.com/product-category/php-ecommerce-script/">Click here</a></strong></p>
